   $('.next_news').click(function (e) {
     e.preventDefault();
     $('.well-flyOutNews').slideToggle("slow");
     $('.next_news').toggleClass('next_news_active');
     if( $('.next_news').hasClass('next_news_active') ) {
       $('.next_news').find('i').removeClass('fa-angle-down').addClass('fa-angle-up');

 $('.boxSmallWhite a').each(function()
 	{
 		var url = $(this).attr('href');
 		var $this = $(this);
 		var contentWell = $(this).parents().eq(4);
 		var h4 = contentWell.prev();
 		
 		contentWell.css('cursor', 'pointer');
 		contentWell.click({url: url}, function(){ 
 			//window.location.href = url;
                         window.open('', $this.attr('target')).location.href = url;
 		});
 		
 		h4.css('cursor', 'pointer');
 		h4.click({url: url}, function(){ 
 			//window.location.href = url;
                         window.open('',$this.attr('target')).location.href = url;
 		});
 	});
 
     
         $('input, textarea').placeholder();
 
 
 
 });

    $(document).ready(function () {
   $('.next_news').click(function (e) {
     e.preventDefault();
     $('.well-flyOutNews').slideToggle("slow");
     $('.next_news').toggleClass('next_news_active');
     if( $('.next_news').hasClass('next_news_active') ) {
       $('.next_news').find('i').removeClass('fa-angle-down').addClass('fa-angle-up');
     } else {
       $('.next_news').find('i').removeClass('fa-angle-up').addClass('fa-angle-down');
     }
   });

 //Add link to the box-white box
 $('.boxSmallWhite a').each(function()
 	{
 		var url = $(this).attr('href');
 		var $this = $(this);
 		var contentWell = $(this).parents().eq(4);
 		var h4 = contentWell.prev();
 		
 		contentWell.css('cursor', 'pointer');
 		contentWell.click({url: url}, function(){ 
 			//window.location.href = url;
                         window.open('', $this.attr('target')).location.href = url;
 		});
 		
 		h4.css('cursor', 'pointer');
 		h4.click({url: url}, function(){ 
 			//window.location.href = url;
                         window.open('',$this.attr('target')).location.href = url;
 		});
 	});
 
     
         $('input, textarea').placeholder();
 
 
 
 });

 	if($('#topperformers_carousel').length){
 		$('#topperformers_carousel').carousel();

   $('.next_news').click(function (e) {
     e.preventDefault();
     $('.well-flyOutNews').slideToggle("slow");
     $('.next_news').toggleClass('next_news_active');
     if( $('.next_news').hasClass('next_news_active') ) {
       $('.next_news').find('i').removeClass('fa-angle-down').addClass('fa-angle-up');

 $('.boxSmallWhite a').each(function()
 	{
 		var url = $(this).attr('href');
 		var $this = $(this);
 		var contentWell = $(this).parents().eq(4);
 		var h4 = contentWell.prev();
 		
 		contentWell.css('cursor', 'pointer');
 		contentWell.click({url: url}, function(){ 
 			//window.location.href = url;
                         window.open('', $this.attr('target')).location.href = url;
 		});
 		
 		h4.css('cursor', 'pointer');
 		h4.click({url: url}, function(){ 
 			//window.location.href = url;
                         window.open('',$this.attr('target')).location.href = url;
 		});
 	});
 
     
         $('input, textarea').placeholder();
 
 
 
 });

    $(document).ready(function () {
   $('.next_news').click(function (e) {
     e.preventDefault();
     $('.well-flyOutNews').slideToggle("slow");
     $('.next_news').toggleClass('next_news_active');
     if( $('.next_news').hasClass('next_news_active') ) {
       $('.next_news').find('i').removeClass('fa-angle-down').addClass('fa-angle-up');
     } else {
       $('.next_news').find('i').removeClass('fa-angle-up').addClass('fa-angle-down');
     }
   });

 //Add link to the box-white box
 $('.boxSmallWhite a').each(function()
 	{
 		var url = $(this).attr('href');
 		var $this = $(this);
 		var contentWell = $(this).parents().eq(4);
 		var h4 = contentWell.prev();
 		
 		contentWell.css('cursor', 'pointer');
 		contentWell.click({url: url}, function(){ 
 			//window.location.href = url;
                         window.open('', $this.attr('target')).location.href = url;
 		});
 		
 		h4.css('cursor', 'pointer');
 		h4.click({url: url}, function(){ 
 			//window.location.href = url;
                         window.open('',$this.attr('target')).location.href = url;
 		});
 	});
 
     
         $('input, textarea').placeholder();
 
 
 
 });

 	if($('#topperformers_carousel').length){
 		$('#topperformers_carousel').carousel();

    $(document).ready(function () {
   $('.next_news').click(function (e) {
     e.preventDefault();
     $('.well-flyOutNews').slideToggle("slow");
     $('.next_news').toggleClass('next_news_active');
     if( $('.next_news').hasClass('next_news_active') ) {
       $('.next_news').find('i').removeClass('fa-angle-down').addClass('fa-angle-up');
     } else {
       $('.next_news').find('i').removeClass('fa-angle-up').addClass('fa-angle-down');
     }
   });
 });
   </script>

 	$('.mainMenu > ul > li').hover(function () {

 		}, function () {
 		$.data(this, 'timer', setTimeout($.proxy(function() {

 //Add link to the box-white box
 $('.boxSmallWhite a').each(function()
 	{
 		var url = $(this).attr('href');
 		var $this = $(this);
 		var contentWell = $(this).parents().eq(4);
 		var h4 = contentWell.prev();
 		
 		contentWell.css('cursor', 'pointer');
 		contentWell.click({url: url}, function(){ 
 			//window.location.href = url;
                         window.open('', $this.attr('target')).location.href = url;
 		});
 		
 		h4.css('cursor', 'pointer');
 		h4.click({url: url}, function(){ 
 			//window.location.href = url;
                         window.open('',$this.attr('target')).location.href = url;
 		});
 	});
 
     
         $('input, textarea').placeholder();
 
 
 
 });
 
 $(document).ready(function(){
 	if($('#topperformers_carousel').length){
 		$('#topperformers_carousel').carousel();
 	}
 });
